%TOAR
% Patterns defined by David Gabay
% 1 - female suffix H 
% 2 - female suffix T 
% 3 - female suffix T, or H or IH if word ends with I 
% 4 - female suffix IT
% 5 - female and male forms are the same
% 6 - female suffix IH
%10 - in the female form the suffix IT replaces H: e.g. NLWWH->NLWWIT
%15 - the femake does not exist, or it is an exception.
